clare my determination as set out in the Schedule a ppended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of  Land Nos. 81, 82, 356, 357, 358, 
359, 360, 361, 362, 363, 364 and 365 of Block 05, co ntained in the Cadastral Map No. 520201, situated in  the Village of Rawatawatta

of Colombo, in the Province of Western, referred to in Notice No. 52/0046 calling for claims to land pa rcels which was duly published 
in the Gazette No. 1580/11 of 17th December, 2008 in terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998.
